To implement the comprehensive accounting system for Al-Nokhba for Electronics, we will use the Django framework for the backend and React.js for the frontend. The database will be MySQL, and the application will be hosted on an Ubuntu server. Below is a step-by-step outline of the core components of the system, followed by the implementation of each component.

### Core Components

1. **Django Backend**
   - **Models**: Define the database schema.
     - `Account`: Represents general ledger accounts.
     - `Invoice`: Represents invoices.
     - `Purchase`: Represents purchase records.
     - `InventoryItem`: Represents inventory items.
     - `FinancialReport`: Represents financial reports.
     - `UserRole`: Represents user roles and permissions.
   - **Views**: Handle HTTP requests and responses.
     - `account_view`: Manage accounts.
     - `invoice_view`: Manage invoices.
     - `purchase_view`: Manage purchases.
     - `inventory_view`: Manage inventory.
     - `report_view`: Generate financial reports.
     - `user_role_view`: Manage user roles.
   - **Serializers**: Convert complex data types to JSON.
   - **URLs**: Route URLs to views.

2. **React Frontend**
   - **Components**: Build the user interface.
     - `AccountComponent`: Interface for managing accounts.
     - `InvoiceComponent`: Interface for managing invoices.
     - `PurchaseComponent`: Interface for managing purchases.
     - `InventoryComponent`: Interface for managing inventory.
     - `ReportComponent`: Interface for generating reports.
     - `UserRoleComponent`: Interface for managing user roles.

3. **Database**
   - **MySQL**: Store all data related to the accounting system.

4. **Deployment**
   - **Ubuntu Server**: Host the application.

### Implementation

#### Django Backend

**models.py**

```python
'''

Defines the database models for the accounting system.

'''

from django.db import models

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class UserRole(models.Model):
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    permissions = models.TextField()

```

**views.py**

```python
'''

Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.

'''

from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer

class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer

class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer

class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer

class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer

class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer

class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer

```

**serializers.py**

```python
'''

Serializes the models for the accounting system.

'''

from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole

class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'

class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'

class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'

class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'

class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'

class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'

```

**urls.py**

```python
'''

Defines URL routing for the accounting system.

'''

from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet

router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)

urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]

```

#### React Frontend

**App.js**

```javascript
'''

Main entry point for the React application.

'''

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';

function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}

export default App;

```

**components/AccountComponent.js**

```javascript
'''

Component for managing accounts.

'''

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default AccountComponent;

```

**components/InvoiceComponent.js**

```javascript
'''

Component for managing invoices.

'''

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default InvoiceComponent;

```

### Deployment

To deploy this application on an Ubuntu server, you will need to:

1. Set up a MySQL database and configure the Django application to connect to it.
2. Install necessary packages and dependencies for both Django and React.
3. Use a web server like Nginx or Apache to serve the Django application.
4. Use a tool like Gunicorn to run the Django application.
5. Build the React application and serve it using a static file server.

This setup provides a comprehensive accounting system with a robust backend and a dynamic frontend, meeting the requirements specified by the customer.

Defines the database models for the accounting system.

from django.db import models

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class UserRole(models.Model):
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    permissions = models.TextField()

+'''
+Component for managing accounts.
+'''
+import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
+import axios from 'axios';
+function AccountComponent() {
+  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
+  useEffect(() => {
+    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
+      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
+      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
+  }, []);
+  return (
+    <div>
+      <h1>Accounts</h1>
+      <ul>
+        {accounts.map(account => (
+          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
+        ))}
+      </ul>
+    </div>
+  );
+}
+export default AccountComponent;

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class UserRole(models.Model):
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    permissions = models.TextField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'
class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]
```

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

'''
Component for managing invoices.

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;

    axios.get('/api/reports/')

      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching reports:', error));

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class UserRole(models.Model):
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    permissions = models.TextField()
```

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;
```

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {
  const [purchases, setPurchases] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Purchases</h1>
      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (
          <li key={purchase.id}>{purchase.item}: {purchase.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default PurchaseComponent;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function ReportComponent() {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/reports/')
      .then(response => setReports(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching reports:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Financial Reports</h1>
      <ul>
        {reports.map(report => (
          <li key={report.id}>{report.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function UserRoleComponent() {
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/userroles/')
      .then(response => setRoles(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching user roles:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>User Roles</h1>
      <ul>
        {roles.map(role => (
          <li key={role.id}>{role.role_name}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default UserRoleComponent;

The `UserRole` model currently stores permissions as a `TextField`, which is not ideal for managing permissions securely and effectively. Instead, consider using Django's built-in `Group` and `Permission` models to manage user roles and permissions. This approach will provide a more robust and secure way to handle user permissions.

### Suggested Revision:
1. **Use Django's Built-in Permissions System:**
   - Replace the `UserRole` model with Django's built-in `Group` and `Permission` models.
   - Assign permissions to groups and users using Django's admin interface or programmatically.

2. **Update Views and Serializers:**
   - Modify the views and serializers to work with the updated user roles and permissions system.

3. **Implement Authentication and Authorization:**
   - Ensure that the application includes authentication (e.g., using Django's authentication system) and restrict access to views based on user roles and permissions.

By implementing these changes, you will enhance the security and maintainability of the application, ensuring that user roles and permissions are managed effectively."

'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js
```javascript
'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default InvoiceComponent;
```

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]
```

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js

'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Purchases</h1>
      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (
          <li key={purchase.id}>{purchase.item}: {purchase.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

import axios from 'axios';
function InventoryComponent() {
  const [inventory, setInventory] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/inventory/')
      .then(response => setInventory(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching inventory:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Inventory</h1>
      <ul>

'''
Component for generating financial reports.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function ReportComponent() {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/reports/')
      .then(response => setReports(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching reports:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Financial Reports</h1>
      <ul>
        {reports.map(report => (
          <li key={report.id}>{report.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default ReportComponent;

userrolecomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing user roles.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function UserRoleComponent() {
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/userroles/')
      .then(response => setRoles(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching user roles:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>User Roles</h1>
      <ul>
        {roles.map(role => (
          <li key={role.id}>{role.role_name}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default UserRoleComponent;

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

'''

from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;
```

'''
Component for managing purchases.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {
  const [purchases, setPurchases] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Purchases</h1>
      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (
          <li key={purchase.id}>{purchase.item}: {purchase.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default PurchaseComponent;
```

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InventoryComponent() {
  const [inventory, setInventory] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/inventory/')
      .then(response => setInventory(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching inventory:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Inventory</h1>
      <ul>
        {inventory.map(item => (
          <li key={item.id}>{item.name}: {item.quantity}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InventoryComponent;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function ReportComponent() {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/reports/')
      .then(response => setReports(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching reports:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Financial Reports</h1>
      <ul>
        {reports.map(report => (
          <li key={report.id}>{report.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default ReportComponent;

'''
Component for managing user roles.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function UserRoleComponent() {
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/userroles/')
      .then(response => setRoles(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching user roles:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>User Roles</h1>
      <ul>
        {roles.map(role => (
          <li key={role.id}>{role.role_name}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default UserRoleComponent;

"The code provided is mostly well-structured and follows the task requirements. However, there is a potential issue with the `UserRoleComponent` in the React front-end. The backend does not seem to have an endpoint for user roles, as there is no `UserRole` model or corresponding viewset in the Django application. This will result in a 404 error when trying to fetch user roles from the `/api/userroles/` endpoint.

To fix this, you should:

1. Define a `UserRole` model in `models.py` if user roles are to be managed separately from Django's built-in `User` and `Group` models.
2. Create a corresponding `UserRoleViewSet` in `views.py`.
3. Register the `UserRoleViewSet` in `urls.py` to expose the `/api/userroles/` endpoint.

This will ensure that the user roles feature is fully functional and aligns with the task requirements."

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

'''

from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet

router = DefaultRouter()

router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)

urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';

function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}

export default App;

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default AccountComponent;
```

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function InvoiceComponent() {

  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')

      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

**[Seminar Conclusion]**:

 models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group

class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]

class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group

class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'

class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'

class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'

class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'

class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'

class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet

router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)

urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'
class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]
```

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;
```

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {
  const [purchases, setPurchases] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Purchases</h1>
      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (
          <li key={purchase.id}>{purchase.item}: {purchase.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default PurchaseComponent;

### Suggestions on Revision:
1. **Implement Role-Based Access Control (RBAC):**
   - Utilize Django's built-in permissions framework or a third-party package like `django-guardian` to implement role-based access control.
   - Define permissions for each model and ensure that only users with the appropriate roles can access or modify specific resources.

2. **Update ViewSets:**
   - Modify the `permission_classes` in each ViewSet to include custom permissions that check the user's role before allowing access.
   - Example:
     ```python
     from rest_framework.permissions import BasePermission

     class IsAccountManager(BasePermission):
         def has_permission(self, request, view):
             return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Account Manager').exists()

     class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
         queryset = Account.objects.all()
         serializer_class = AccountSerializer
         permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsAccountManager]
     ```

Task: "Please help me implement a Python web application using Django or Flask to create a comprehensive accounting system for Al-Nokhba for Electronics, which includes features for managing general ledger, invoices, purchases, inventory, financial reports, and user roles, with a front-end developed in HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (Bootstrap), preferably React.js or Vue.js, and MySQL as the database on an Ubuntu server.".

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from django.contrib.auth.models import User, Group
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'
class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;
```

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {
  const [purchases, setPurchases] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>

      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (

  );

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function ReportComponent() {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/reports/')
      .then(response => setReports(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching reports:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Financial Reports</h1>
      <ul>
        {reports.map(report => (
          <li key={report.id}>{report.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function UserRoleComponent() {
  const [roles, setRoles] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/userroles/')
      .then(response => setRoles(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching user roles:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>User Roles</h1>
      <ul>
        {roles.map(role => (
          <li key={role.id}>{role.role_name}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default UserRoleComponent;

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User

class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()

class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()

class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
from rest_framework.permissions import BasePermission

class IsAccountManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Account Manager').exists()

class IsInvoiceManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Invoice Manager').exists()

class IsPurchaseManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Purchase Manager').exists()

class IsInventoryManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Inventory Manager').exists()

class IsReportManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Report Manager').exists()

class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsAccountManager]

class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsInvoiceManager]

class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsPurchaseManager]

class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsInventoryManager]

class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsReportManager]

class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole

class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'

class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'

class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'

class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'

class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'

class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'

"models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for the accounting system.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
class Account(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    balance = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
class Invoice(models.Model):
    account = models.ForeignKey(Account, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class Purchase(models.Model):
    item = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    date = models.DateField()
class InventoryItem(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    quantity = models.IntegerField()
class FinancialReport(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class UserRole(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    role_name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests and responses for the accounting system.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import viewsets, permissions
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
from .serializers import AccountSerializer, InvoiceSerializer, PurchaseSerializer, InventoryItemSerializer, FinancialReportSerializer, UserRoleSerializer
from rest_framework.permissions import BasePermission
class IsAccountManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Account Manager').exists()
class IsInvoiceManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Invoice Manager').exists()
class IsPurchaseManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Purchase Manager').exists()
class IsInventoryManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Inventory Manager').exists()
class IsReportManager(BasePermission):
    def has_permission(self, request, view):
        return request.user.userrole_set.filter(role_name='Report Manager').exists()
class AccountViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Account.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AccountSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsAccountManager]
class InvoiceViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Invoice.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InvoiceSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsInvoiceManager]
class PurchaseViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Purchase.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PurchaseSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsPurchaseManager]
class InventoryItemViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = InventoryItem.objects.all()
    serializer_class = InventoryItemSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsInventoryManager]
class FinancialReportViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = FinancialReport.objects.all()
    serializer_class = FinancialReportSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated, IsReportManager]
class UserRoleViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = UserRole.objects.all()
    serializer_class = UserRoleSerializer
    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]
```

serializers.py
```python
'''
Serializes the models for the accounting system.
'''
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Account, Invoice, Purchase, InventoryItem, FinancialReport, UserRole
class AccountSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Account
        fields = '__all__'
class InvoiceSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Invoice
        fields = '__all__'
class PurchaseSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Purchase
        fields = '__all__'
class InventoryItemSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = InventoryItem
        fields = '__all__'
class FinancialReportSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = FinancialReport
        fields = '__all__'
class UserRoleSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = UserRole
        fields = '__all__'
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the accounting system.
'''
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from .views import AccountViewSet, InvoiceViewSet, PurchaseViewSet, InventoryItemViewSet, FinancialReportViewSet, UserRoleViewSet
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'accounts', AccountViewSet)
router.register(r'invoices', InvoiceViewSet)
router.register(r'purchases', PurchaseViewSet)
router.register(r'inventory', InventoryItemViewSet)
router.register(r'reports', FinancialReportViewSet)
router.register(r'userroles', UserRoleViewSet)
urlpatterns = [
    path('', include(router.urls)),
]
```

app.js
```js
'''
Main entry point for the React application.
'''
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import AccountComponent from './components/AccountComponent';
import InvoiceComponent from './components/InvoiceComponent';
import PurchaseComponent from './components/PurchaseComponent';
import InventoryComponent from './components/InventoryComponent';
import ReportComponent from './components/ReportComponent';
import UserRoleComponent from './components/UserRoleComponent';
function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Switch>
        <Route path="/accounts" component={AccountComponent} />
        <Route path="/invoices" component={InvoiceComponent} />
        <Route path="/purchases" component={PurchaseComponent} />
        <Route path="/inventory" component={InventoryComponent} />
        <Route path="/reports" component={ReportComponent} />
        <Route path="/userroles" component={UserRoleComponent} />
      </Switch>
    </Router>
  );
}
export default App;
```

accountcomponent.js
```js
'''
Component for managing accounts.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function AccountComponent() {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/accounts/')
      .then(response => setAccounts(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching accounts:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Accounts</h1>
      <ul>
        {accounts.map(account => (
          <li key={account.id}>{account.name}: {account.balance}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default AccountComponent;
```

invoicecomponent.js

'''
Component for managing invoices.
'''
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function InvoiceComponent() {
  const [invoices, setInvoices] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/invoices/')
      .then(response => setInvoices(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching invoices:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Invoices</h1>
      <ul>
        {invoices.map(invoice => (
          <li key={invoice.id}>{invoice.account.name}: {invoice.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default InvoiceComponent;
```

import axios from 'axios';
function PurchaseComponent() {
  const [purchases, setPurchases] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    axios.get('/api/purchases/')
      .then(response => setPurchases(response.data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching purchases:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Purchases</h1>
      <ul>
        {purchases.map(purchase => (
          <li key={purchase.id}>{purchase.item}: {purchase.amount}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default PurchaseComponent;
